Here are the results of the ANOVA tests for each player:

   - p-value: 0.102

   - Interpretation: Borderline significant seasonal pattern (p is close to 0.05).

   - p-value: 0.046
   - Interpretation: Significant seasonal pattern (since p < 0.05).

4. **Donald Forrester:**

   - p-value: 0.781
   - Interpretation: No significant seasonal pattern (since p > 0.05).

### Interpretation:
- **John King** shows a significant seasonal pattern in his Wordle scores across different months.
- **Ian Wakeman** shows a borderline significant seasonal pattern.
- **Stephen Macaulay** and **Donald Forrester** do not show significant seasonal patterns.

24/08/2024, 12:49 - John King: Fun fact... When someone has had a brain injury, we want to find out what their IQ was beforehand. It's very difficult obviously, but one of the best ways we do have is asking people to pronounce a list of unusual words (the NART test). This is because our lexical knowledge is so embedded that it's quite resistant to damage.

But it's also highly correlated with having more years of education, being a big reader, and being posh.

06/06/2025, 11:06 - John King: Have you gone direct to the Credit Reference Agencies? (Experian, Equifax, TransUnion, Submit online (Experian → “Add a Notice of Correction”; Equifax → “ADD A NOTICE OF CORRECTION”; TransUnion → email form). 
help.equifax.co.uk
transunion.co.uk

Keep the text very short, e.g.:

“I request that no credit be granted unless the applicant quotes the password MERLIN2025.”

Lenders are contractually obliged to read NOCs, but a fully automated lender that cannot handle the manual step may simply decline rather than contact you.
06/06/2025, 11:07 - John King: Also this:

Cifas Protective Registration

Apply direct at cifas.org.uk; you will need proof of identity and payment (£30). 
cifas.org.uk

The marker is visible to all Cifas members, not just the three credit reference agencies, so it also covers telecoms contracts and some online-only accounts.

Because extra checks are triggered, applications can take days rather than minutes, and — as recent ombudsman cases show — some lenders erroneously treat the flag as a reason to reject.

08/06/2025, 09:01 - John King: Learn to use a password manager. I use Bitwarden. It's an app on my phone and browser plugin on my laptop. It means I have different unique, long uncrackable passwords on every account.

Never ignore messages from your phone company, if anyone tries to take your number, you will get text messages about it including the term "PAC" - port authorisation code

Have all bank accounts set to inform you by text of any transactions

Avoid enabling text messages as a form of validation. Use authenticator apps instead. This is not always possible.

06/07/2025, 08:42 - Ian Wakeman: Renowned AI Expert Prof. Ian Wakeman Visited ZJSU
On the morning of June 24 , Prof. Ian Wakeman, an internationally acclaimed artificial intelligence expert and Professor of Informatics at the University of Sussex visited Zhejiang Gongshang University (ZJSU). Prof. Yu Jianxing, Secretary of the University Party Committee, met with the distinguished guest. During the meeting, Prof. Yu warmly congratulated Prof. Wakeman on receiving the "West Lake Friendship Award" from the Zhejiang Provincial Government and presented him with the "Outstanding Contribution Award for Sino-Foreign Cooperative Education at ZJSU". The meeting was attended by representatives from the International Office and the School of Information and Electronic Engineering ( ZJSU-Sussex AI Joint Institute).

Prof. Yu expressed sincere gratitude for Prof.Wakeman’s exceptional contributions to the establishment and development of the ZJSU-Sussex AI Institute. He particularly highlighted Prof. Wakeman’s decades of dedication, intellectual rigor, and selfless commitment, which have laid a solid foundation for the in-depth collaboration between the two institutions. Prof. Yu expressed hope that Prof. Wakeman would continue supporting the institute’s growth, helping ZJSU cultivate globally competitive AI talents and produce more groundbreaking research outcomes.

Prof. Wakeman reflected on his rewarding journey in co-establishing the joint institute and praised the remarkable achievements made through the partnership. He noted that ZJSU’s rapid advancements in AI and its open, innovative academic environment left a profound impression. Moving forward, both universities will strengthen collaboration in AI education, research, and discipline development, jointly exploring cutting-edge challenges in the field.



Prof. Wakeman’s West Lake Friendship Award signifies a milestone in ZJSU’s efforts to attract global academic leaders and enhance the international competitiveness of its AI disciplines. It also underscores the outstanding contributions of foreign experts to Zhejiang’s educational and technological progress. This achievement will further deepen the strategic partnership between the Chinese and British institutions, providing core support for building a world-class AI teaching and research team and contributing ZJSU’s expertise to regional and national AI industry development.
